## Domain Knowledge (LLM-generated)
**Domain**: population ecology / population dynamics
**Analysis**: This task models the population growth rate dP/dt as a function of time t and population P, which is the core problem of population dynamics. The relationship likely involves density-dependent growth terms where the growth rate depends on population size, possibly with time-varying parameters.

**Common formula structures in this domain**:
- Exponential growth: dP_dt = c0 * P (density-independent unlimited growth)
- Logistic growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) (density-dependent growth with carrying capacity)
- Gompertz growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * log(c1 / P) (growth decelerating logarithmically near carrying capacity)
- Theta-logistic: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2) (generalized logistic with shape parameter)
- Allee effect (strong): dP_dt = c0 * P * (P * c1 - 1) * (1 - c2 * P) (growth negative below critical population threshold)
- Allee effect (weak): dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) * (c2 + P) (reduced growth at low density without critical threshold)
- Beverton-Holt continuous: dP_dt = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (saturating per-capita growth rate)
- Time-varying carrying capacity logistic: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P * exp(c2 * t)) (logistic with exponentially shifting capacity)
- Harvesting/mortality logistic: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) - c2 * P (logistic growth with proportional harvesting)
- Constant harvesting logistic: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) - c2 (logistic growth with constant harvesting rate)
- Richards growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2) (flexible asymmetric sigmoid growth)
- Quadratic density dependence: dP_dt = c0 * P + c1 * P**2 + c2 * P**3 (polynomial density-dependent growth)
- Time-modulated growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) * (1 + c2 * sin(c3 * t)) (logistic with seasonal variation)
- Power-law growth: dP_dt = c0 * P**c1 (fractional power density dependence)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Density-dependent negative feedback → quadratic term -c*P^2 or rational form P/(1+c*P), indicating competition for limited resources
- Allee effect (positive density dependence at low P) → cubic structure with two positive roots: P*(P-a)*(K-P), producing negative growth below critical threshold
- Per-capita growth rate declining linearly with P → dP/dt has P and P^2 terms (logistic signature)
- Seasonal or periodic environmental forcing → multiplicative sinusoidal modulation (1 + c*sin(ω*t)) on growth terms
- Carrying capacity as a separable factor → growth rate vanishes at specific P value, look for (1 - c*P) or log(c/P) factors
- Time-dependent parameters → exponential or polynomial functions of t multiplied by population-dependent terms, indicating environmental change
- Depensation/extinction threshold → growth rate sign change at small P, requiring multiplicative factor (P - c) with c > 0
- Immigration/emigration → additive constant term independent of P, shifting the zero-growth isocline
